````
<skill_content name="openspec-explore">
# Skill: openspec-explore

Enter explore mode. Think deeply. Visualize freely. Follow the conversation wherever it goes.

**IMPORTANT: Explore mode is for thinking, not implementing.** You may read files, search code, and investigate the codebase, but you must NEVER write code or implement features. If the user asks you to implement something, remind them to exit explore mode first (e.g., start a change with `/opsx:new` or `/opsx:ff`). You MAY create OpenSpec artifacts (proposals, designs, specs) if the user asks—that's capturing thinking, not implementing.

**This is a stance, not a workflow.** There are no fixed steps, no required sequence, no mandatory outputs. You're a thinking partner helping the user explore.

---

## The Stance

- **Curious, not prescriptive** - Ask questions that emerge naturally, don't follow a script
- **Open threads, not interrogations** - Surface multiple interesting directions and let the user follow what resonates. Don't funnel them through a single path of questions.
- **Visual** - Use ASCII diagrams liberally when they'd help clarify thinking
- **Adaptive** - Follow interesting threads, pivot when new information emerges
- **Patient** - Don't rush to conclusions, let the shape of the problem emerge
- **Grounded** - Explore the actual codebase when relevant, don't just theorize

---

## What You Might Do

Depending on what the user brings, you might:

**Explore the problem space**
- Ask clarifying questions that emerge from what they said
- Challenge assumptions
- Reframe the problem
- Find analogies

**Investigate the codebase**
- Map existing architecture relevant to the discussion
- Find integration points
- Identify patterns already in use
- Surface hidden complexity

**Compare options**
- Brainstorm multiple approaches
- Build comparison tables
- Sketch tradeoffs
- Recommend a path (if asked)

**Visualize**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│     Use ASCII diagrams liberally        │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                         │
│   ┌────────┐         ┌────────┐        │
│   │ State  │────────▶│ State  │        │
│   │   A    │         │   B    │        │
│   └────────┘         └────────┘        │
│                                         │
│   System diagrams, state machines,      │
│   data flows, architecture sketches,    │
│   dependency graphs, comparison tables  │
│                                         │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Surface risks and unknowns**
- Identify what could go wrong
- Find gaps in understanding
- Suggest spikes or investigations

---

## OpenSpec Awareness

You have full context of the OpenSpec system. Use it naturally, don't force it.

### Check for context

At the start, quickly check what exists:
```bash
openspec list --json
```

This tells you:
- If there are active changes
- Their names, schemas, and status
- What the user might be working on

### When no change exists

Think freely. When insights crystallize, you might offer:

- "This feels solid enough to start a change. Want me to create one?"
  → Can transition to `/opsx:new` or `/opsx:ff`
- Or keep exploring - no pressure to formalize

### When a change exists

If the user mentions a change or you detect one is relevant:

1. **Read existing artifacts for context**
   - `openspec/changes/<name>/proposal.md`
   - `openspec/changes/<name>/design.md`
   - `openspec/changes/<name>/tasks.md`
   - etc.

2. **Reference them naturally in conversation**
   - "Your design mentions using Redis, but we just realized SQLite fits better..."
   - "The proposal scopes this to premium users, but we're now thinking everyone..."

3. **Offer to capture when decisions are made**

   | Insight Type | Where to Capture |
   |--------------|------------------|
   | New requirement discovered | `specs/<capability>/spec.md` |
   | Requirement changed | `specs/<capability>/spec.md` |
   | Design decision made | `design.md` |
   | Scope changed | `proposal.md` |
   | New work identified | `tasks.md` |
   | Assumption invalidated | Relevant artifact |

   Example offers:
   - "That's a design decision. Capture it in design.md?"
   - "This is a new requirement. Add it to specs?"
   - "This changes scope. Update the proposal?"

4. **The user decides** - Offer and move on. Don't pressure. Don't auto-capture.

---

## What You Don't Have To Do

- Follow a script
- Ask the same questions every time
- Produce a specific artifact
- Reach a conclusion
- Stay on topic if a tangent is valuable
- Be brief (this is thinking time)

## Ending Discovery

There's no required ending. Discovery might:

- **Flow into action**: "Ready to start? /opsx:new or /opsx:ff"
- **Result in artifact updates**: "Updated design.md with these decisions"
- **Just provide clarity**: User has what they need, moves on
- **Continue later**: "We can pick this up anytime"

When it feels like things are crystallizing, you might summarize:

```
## What We Figured Out

**The problem**: [crystallized understanding]

**The approach**: [if one emerged]

**Open questions**: [if any remain]

**Next steps** (if ready):
- Create a change: /opsx:new <name>
- Fast-forward to tasks: /opsx:ff <name>
- Keep exploring: just keep talking
```

But this summary is optional. Sometimes the thinking IS the value.

- **Don't rush** - Discovery is thinking time, not task time

- **Don't auto-capture** - Offer to save insights, don't just do it
- **Do visualize** - A good diagram is worth many paragraphs
- **Do explore the codebase** - Ground discussions in reality
- **Do question assumptions** - Including the user's and your own
````

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # MIMO Platform
2: 
3: A minimal, Emacs-style web-based editor for AI-assisted development.
4: 
5: ## Overview
6: 
7: MIMO (Minimal IDE for Modern Operations) is a platform that enables AI-assisted development through a web-based interface with an Emacs-style workflow. It provides session-based development with worktrees, file synchronization, and integrated chat with AI agents.
8: 
9: ## Features
10: 
11: - **Public Landing Page**: View platform overview and public projects without authentication
12: - **Project Descriptions**: Add optional descriptions to projects for better discoverability
13: - **Emacs-Style Interface**: Three-buffer layout with customizable keybindings
14: - **Session-Based Development**: Work with isolated worktrees for each development session
15: - **File Synchronization**: Automatic sync between agent worktree and original repository
16: - **Integrated Chat**: Real-time chat with AI agents via WebSocket
17: - **VCS Integration**: Fossil as intermediary for both Git and Fossil repositories
18: - **Agent Lifecycle**: Spawn and manage AI agents with JWT authentication
19: - **Conflict Detection**: Smart conflict detection with baseline checksums
20: 
21: ## Architecture
22: 
23: ```
24: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
25: │                      Browser (Client)                       │
26: │  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐   │
27: │  │ Files Tree  │  │   Chat      │  │    Changes      │   │
28: │  │   (Left)    │  │  (Center)   │  │    (Right)      │   │
29: │  └─────────────┘  └─────────────┘  └─────────────────┘   │
30: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
31:                           │ WebSocket / HTTP
32: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
33: │                 mimo-platform (Hono/Bun)                   │
34: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
35: │  │  Auth  │  Projects  │  Sessions  │  Agents  │ Sync │  │
36: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
37: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
38: │  │              WebSocket Handlers                      │  │
39: │  │         (Chat, Agent Connections)                  │  │
40: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
41: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
42:                           │
43: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
44: │                   mimo-agent (Binary)                      │
45: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
46: │  │         File Watcher  │  ACP Process Proxy        │  │
47: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
48: └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
49: ```
50: 
51: ## Installation
52: 
53: ### Prerequisites
54: 
55: - [Bun](https://bun.sh) 1.0+
56: - [Fossil](https://fossil-scm.org) 2.27+
57: - Git (for Git repository support)
58: 
59: ### Quick Start
60: 
61: ```bash
62: # Clone the repository
63: git clone https://github.com/your-org/mimo.git
64: cd mimo
65: 
66: # Install dependencies
67: cd packages/mimo-platform
68: bun install
69: 
70: # Start the server
71: bun run dev
72: ```
73: 
74: The platform will be available at `http://localhost:3000`
75: 
76: ### Build the Agent
77: 
78: ```bash
79: cd packages/mimo-agent
80: bun install
81: bun run build
82: ```
83: 
84: This creates `dist/mimo-agent` which is used by the platform.
85: 
86: ## Usage
87: 
88: ### Public Landing Page
89: 
90: When you first navigate to `http://localhost:3000`, you'll see a public landing page displaying:
91: - Platform overview and features
92: - List of all public projects (names, descriptions, owners, repo types)
93: - Login and Register buttons
94: 
95: Clicking on a project card will redirect you to login if not authenticated, or take you directly to the project detail if authenticated.
96: 
97: ### Authentication
98: 
99: 1. Navigate to `http://localhost:3000/auth/register`
100: 2. Create an account
101: 3. Login at `http://localhost:3000/auth/login`
102: 
103: ### Creating a Project
104: 
105: 1. Click "Create Project" on the projects page
106: 2. Enter project name
107: 3. Add an optional description (recommended ~200 chars, max 500)
108: 4. Provide Git or Fossil repository URL
109: 5. The system imports/clones the repository
110: 
111: ### Starting a Session
112: 
113: 1. Select a project from the projects list
114: 2. Click "New Session"
115: 3. Enter session name
116: 4. The system sets up a Fossil worktree
117: 
118: ### Working with Agents
119: 
120: 1. In a session, click "Start Agent"
121: 2. The platform spawns an agent process
122: 3. Chat with the agent in the center buffer
123: 4. File changes appear in the right buffer automatically
124: 
125: ### Committing Changes
126: 
127: 1. Make changes through the agent
128: 2. Click "Commit" button or press `C-x c`
129: 3. Enter commit message
130: 4. Changes are committed to Fossil and pushed to the original repository
131: 
132: ## Configuration
133: 
134: Configuration is stored in `~/.mimo/config.yaml`:
135: 
136: ```yaml
137: theme: dark
138: fontSize: 14
139: fontFamily: monospace
140: keybindings:
141:   cancel_request: "C-c C-c"
142:   commit: "C-x c"
143:   find_file: "C-x C-f"
144:   switch_project: "C-x p"
145:   switch_session: "C-x s"
146:   focus_left: "C-x h"
147:   focus_center: "C-x j"
148:   focus_right: "C-x l"
149: ```
150: 
151: Edit via the web UI at `/config` or directly in the file.
152: 
153: ## Directory Structure
154: 
155: ```
156: ~/.mimo/
157: ├── config.yaml           # User configuration
158: ├── users/
159: │   └── {username}/
160: │       └── credentials.yaml
161: ├── projects/
162: │   └── {project-id}/
163: │       ├── project.yaml
164: │       ├── repo.fossil
165: │       ├── original/     # Original repo worktree
166: │       └── sessions/
167: │           └── {session-id}/
168: │               ├── session.yaml
169: │               ├── chat.jsonl
170: │               ├── repo.fossil       # Fossil proxy for agent sync
171: │               ├── upstream/         # Original repository clone
172: │               └── agent-workspace/  # Agent working directory (plain files)
173: └── agents/
174:     └── {agent-id}/
175:         └── agent.yaml
176: ```
177: 
178: ### Session Directory Structure
179: 
180: Each session directory contains:
181: 
182: - `session.yaml` - Session metadata (name, status, port, agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath)
183: - `chat.jsonl` - Chat message history
184: - `repo.fossil` - Fossil proxy repository for agent synchronization
185: - `upstream/` - Clone of the original repository (Git or Fossil)
186: - `agent-workspace/` - Working directory where agent makes edits (plain files, not a repository)
187: 
188: **Note:** The `agent-workspace/` was previously called `checkout/` but was renamed to clarify its purpose as a working directory rather than a repository checkout.
189: 
190: ## Commit and Push Flow
191: 
192: When you click "Commit" in a session, the system performs a 4-step commit flow:
193: 
194: 1. **Sync** (`fossil up`) - Synchronizes the agent-workspace with the latest changes from repo.fossil
195: 2. **Copy** (clean slate) - Copies all files from agent-workspace to upstream/ directory, removing old files
196: 3. **Commit** - Commits changes in the upstream/ directory with message "Mimo commit at <timestamp>"
197: 4. **Push** - Pushes the commit to the remote repository
198: 
199: The commit flow preserves VCS metadata (`.git/` or `.fossil`) during the copy operation.
200: 
201: ### Breaking Changes
202: 
203: **Old sessions need recreation**: Sessions created before the agent-workspace rename (v1.x) stored `checkoutPath` in session.yaml. These sessions will need to be recreated to work with the new commit flow.
204: 
205: ## Development
206: 
207: ```bash
208: # Run tests
209: bun test
210: 
211: # Run with hot reload
212: bun run dev
213: 
214: # Build for production
215: bun run build
216: ```
217: 
218: ## License
219: 
220: MIT License - see LICENSE file for details.
221: 
222: ## Contributing
223: 
224: Contributions are welcome! Please read CONTRIBUTING.md for guidelines.

(End of file - total 224 lines)
</content>
````

```
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import type { FC } from "hono/jsx";
2: import { Layout } from "./Layout.js";
3: 
4: interface Project {
5:   id: string;
6:   name: string;
7: }
8: 
9: interface Session {
10:   id: string;
11:   name: string;
12:   status: "active" | "paused" | "closed";
13:   upstreamPath: string;
14:   agentWorkspacePath: string;
15:   assignedAgentId?: string;
16:   createdAt: Date;
17: }
18: 
19: interface ChatMessage {
20:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
21:   content: string;
22:   timestamp: string;
23: }
24: 
25: interface Agent {
26:   id: string;
27:   status: "online" | "offline";
28:   startedAt: Date;
29:   lastActivityAt?: Date;
30: }
31: 
32: interface FileChange {
33:   path: string;
34:   status: "clean" | "modified" | "new" | "deleted" | "conflict";
35: }
36: 
37: // Model and Mode selector types
38: interface ModelState {
39:   currentModelId: string;
40:   availableModels: Array<{ value: string; name: string; description?: string }>;
41:   optionId: string;
42: }
43: 
44: interface ModeState {
45:   currentModeId: string;
46:   availableModes: Array<{ value: string; name: string; description?: string }>;
47:   optionId: string;
48: }
49: 
50: interface SessionDetailProps {
51:   project: Project;
52:   session: Session;
53:   chatHistory: ChatMessage[];
54:   agent?: Agent;
55:   changes?: FileChange[];
56:   hasConflicts?: boolean;
57:   modelState?: ModelState;
58:   modeState?: ModeState;
59: }
60: 
61: function renderFileTree(changes: FileChange[]) {
62:   const fileTree: Map<string, { name: string; status: FileChange["status"] }[]> = new Map();
63:   
64:   for (const change of changes) {
65:     const parts = change.path.split("/");
66:     const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
67:     const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
68:     
69:     if (!fileTree.has(dir)) {
70:       fileTree.set(dir, []);
71:     }
72:     fileTree.get(dir)!.push({ name: fileName, status: change.status });
73:   }
74:   
75:   const sortedDirs = Array.from(fileTree.entries()).sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]));
76:   
77:   return (
78:     <div class="file-tree">
79:       {sortedDirs.map(([dir, files]) => (
80:         <div key={dir} class="file-tree-dir">
81:           <div class="file-tree-dir-name">{dir}/</div>
82:           <div class="file-tree-files">
83:             {files.map((file) => (
84:               <div key={file.name} class="file-tree-file">
85:                 <span class={`file-indicator file-indicator-${file.status}`}>
86:                   {file.status === "modified" && "[M]"}
87:                   {file.status === "new" && "[?]"}
88:                   {file.status === "deleted" && "[D]"}
89:                   {file.status === "conflict" && "[!]"}
90:                   {file.status === "clean" && "   "}
91:                 </span>
92:                 <span class={`file-name file-name-${file.status}`}>{file.name}</span>
93:               </div>
94:             ))}
95:           </div>
96:         </div>
97:       ))}
98:     </div>
99:   );
100: }
101: 
102: function getStatusIcon(status: FileChange["status"]): string {
103:   switch (status) {
104:     case "modified": return "M";
105:     case "new": return "?";
106:     case "deleted": return "D";
107:     case "conflict": return "!";
108:     default: return " ";
109:   }
110: }
111:

133:                 </span>
```

```
283:   }

292:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
293:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
294:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
295:   
296:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
297:   
298:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
299:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
300:       return;
301:     }
302:     
303:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
304:     
305:     for (const entry of entries) {
306:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
307:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
308:       
309:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
310:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
311:       } else {
312:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
313:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
314:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
315:         
316:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
317:           fileTree[dir] = [];
318:         }
319:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
320:       }
321:     }
322:   }
323:   
324:   try {
325:     scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
326:   } catch (error) {
327:     console.error("Error scanning checkout:", error);
328:   }
329: 
330:   // Return HTML file tree
331:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
332: <html>
333: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
334: <body>
335: <div class="file-tree">
336: `;
337: 
338:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
339:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
340:     for (const file of files) {
341:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
342:     }
343:   }
344: 
345:   html += `</div>
346: </body>
347: </html>`;
348: 
349:   return c.html(html);
350: });
```

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/sync/service.ts

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:27:13
**Parameters:**

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/sync/service.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { join, relative, dirname, resolve } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, copyFileSync, mkdirSync, statSync, readFileSync, readdirSync, unlinkSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: import { sessionRepository } from "../sessions/repository.js";
5: import crypto from "crypto";
6: 
7: export type FileStatus = 
8:   | "clean"      // File hasn't changed
9:   | "modified"   // File modified by agent [M]
10:   | "new"        // New file created by agent [?]
11:   | "deleted"    // File deleted by agent [D]
12:   | "conflict";  // Conflict with original repo [!]
13: 
14: export interface FileChange {
15:   path: string;
16:   status: FileStatus;
17:   timestamp: Date;
18:   checksum?: string;
19:   size?: number;
20:   lastModified?: Date;
21: }
22: 
23: export interface ChangeSet {
24:   sessionId: string;
25:   files: FileChange[];
26:   syncedAt?: Date;
27:   hasConflicts: boolean;
28: }
29: 
30: export interface FileSyncState {
31:   sessionId: string;
32:   upstreamPath: string;
33:   agentWorkspacePath: string;
34:   changes: Map<string, FileChange>;
35:   baselineChecksums: Map<string, string>; // Track original checksums at last sync
36:   lastSyncAt?: Date;
37: }
38: 
39: export class FileSyncService {
40:   private syncStates: Map<string, FileSyncState> = new Map();
41:   private pendingChanges: Map<string, FileChange[]> = new Map(); // Buffered changes for reconnects
42: 
43:   async initializeSession(
44:     sessionId: string,
45:     agentWorkspacePath: string,
46:     upstreamPath?: string
47:   ): Promise<void> {
48:     // Get paths from session if not provided
49:     if (!upstreamPath || !agentWorkspacePath) {
50:       const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
51:       if (!session) {
52:         throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
53:       }
54:       
55:       upstreamPath = upstreamPath || session.upstreamPath;
56:       agentWorkspacePath = agentWorkspacePath || session.agentWorkspacePath;
57:     }
58: 
59:     const syncState: FileSyncState = {
60:       sessionId,
61:       upstreamPath,
62:       agentWorkspacePath,
63:       changes: new Map(),
64:       baselineChecksums: new Map(),
65:     };
66: 
67:     this.syncStates.set(sessionId, syncState);
68:     
69:     // Initialize empty pending changes buffer
70:     this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);
71: 
72:     // Scan current state
73:     await this.scanSessionCheckout(sessionId);
74:   }
75: 
76:   async handleFileChanges(
77:     sessionId: string, 
78:     changes: Array<{ path: string; isNew?: boolean; deleted?: boolean }>
79:   ): Promise<FileChange[]> {
80:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
81:     if (!syncState) {
82:       await this.initializeSession(sessionId, "", "");
83:     }
84: 
85:     const fileChanges: FileChange[] = [];
86: 
87:     for (const change of changes) {
88:       let status: FileStatus = "modified";
89:       
90:       if (change.deleted) {
91:         status = "deleted";
92:       } else if (change.isNew) {
93:         status = "new";
94:       } else {
95:         // Check if file exists in original repo
96:         const originalPath = join(syncState!.upstreamPath, change.path);
97:         const sessionPath = join(syncState!.agentWorkspacePath, change.path);
98:         
99:         if (!existsSync(originalPath) && existsSync(sessionPath)) {
100:           status = "new";
101:         }
102:       }
103: 
104:       // Check for conflicts
105:       const conflictStatus = await this.checkConflict(
106:         sessionId, 
107:         change.path, 
108:         status
109:       );
110: 
111:       const fileChange: FileChange = {
112:         path: change.path,
113:         status: conflictStatus || status,
114:         timestamp: new Date(),
115:         ...(status !== "deleted" && await this.getFileInfo(sessionId, change.path)),
116:       };
117: 
118:       syncState!.changes.set(change.path, fileChange);
119:       fileChanges.push(fileChange);
120:     }
121: 
122:     // Sync changes to original repo
123:     await this.syncChangesToUpstream(sessionId, fileChanges);
124: 
125:     return fileChanges;
126:   }
127: 
128:   private async checkConflict(
129:     sessionId: string,
130:     filePath: string,
131:     agentStatus: FileStatus
132:   ): Promise<FileStatus | null> {
133:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
134:     if (!syncState) return null;
135: 
136:     // Skip conflict check for new files
137:     if (agentStatus === "new") return null;
138: 
139:     const originalPath = join(syncState.upstreamPath, filePath);
140:     
141:     // If file doesn't exist in original, no conflict
142:     if (!existsSync(originalPath)) {
143:       return null;
144:     }
145: 
146:     // Get checksums
147:     const sessionPath = join(syncState.agentWorkspacePath, filePath);
148:     
149:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
150:       // File was deleted in session but exists in original
151:       // Check if original was modified since last sync
152:       const originalChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(originalPath);
153:       const baselineChecksum = syncState.baselineChecksums.get(filePath);
154:       
155:       if (baselineChecksum && originalChecksum !== baselineChecksum) {
156:         return "conflict";
157:       }
158:       return null;
159:     }
160: 
161:     // Compare checksums
162:     const originalChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(originalPath);
163:     const sessionChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(sessionPath);
164:     const baselineChecksum = syncState.baselineChecksums.get(filePath);
165: 
166:     // If original changed since last sync and agent also changed it, it's a conflict
167:     if (baselineChecksum && 
168:         originalChecksum !== baselineChecksum && 
169:         sessionChecksum !== baselineChecksum) {
170:       return "conflict";
171:     }
172: 
173:     return null;
174:   }
175: 
176:   private async syncChangesToUpstream(
177:     sessionId: string, 
178:     changes: FileChange[]
179:   ): Promise<void> {
180:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
181:     if (!syncState) return;
182: 
183:     for (const change of changes) {
184:       if (change.status === "conflict") {
185:         // Don't sync conflicts - require manual resolution
186:         continue;
187:       }
188: 
189:       const sessionPath = join(syncState.agentWorkspacePath, change.path);
190:       const originalPath = join(syncState.upstreamPath, change.path);
191: 
192:       try {
193:         if (change.status === "deleted") {
194:           if (existsSync(originalPath)) {
195:             unlinkSync(originalPath);
196:           }
197:           // Remove from baseline
198:           syncState.baselineChecksums.delete(change.path);
199:         } else if (change.status === "new" || change.status === "modified") {
200:           // Ensure directory exists
201:           const originalDir = dirname(originalPath);
202:           if (!existsSync(originalDir)) {
203:             mkdirSync(originalDir, { recursive: true });
204:           }
205: 
206:           // Copy file with permissions
207:           if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
208:             copyFileSync(sessionPath, originalPath);
209:             
210:             // Preserve timestamps if available
211:             if (change.lastModified) {
212:               const fs = require("fs");
213:               fs.utimesSync(originalPath, change.lastModified, change.lastModified);
214:             }
215:             
216:             // Update baseline checksum
217:             const newChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(sessionPath);
218:             syncState.baselineChecksums.set(change.path, newChecksum);
219:           }
220:         }
221:       } catch (error) {
222:         console.error(`Failed to sync ${change.path}:`, error);
223:       }
224:     }
225: 
226:     // Update last sync time
227:     syncState.lastSyncAt = new Date();
228:   }
229: 
230:   async manualPullFromOriginal(sessionId: string): Promise<FileChange[]> {
231:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
232:     if (!syncState) {
233:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not initialized`);
234:     }
235: 
236:     const changes: FileChange[] = [];
237: 
238:     // Scan original repo for changes
239:     await this.scanDirectory(
240:       syncState.upstreamPath,
241:       syncState.upstreamPath,
242:       async (originalPath, relativePath) => {
243:         const sessionPath = join(syncState.agentWorkspacePath, relativePath);
244:         
245:         // Check if file exists in session
246:         if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
247:           // File exists in original but not in session - copy it
248:           const sessionDir = dirname(sessionPath);
249:           if (!existsSync(sessionDir)) {
250:             mkdirSync(sessionDir, { recursive: true });
251:           }
252:           
253:           copyFileSync(originalPath, sessionPath);
254:           
255:           const fileChange: FileChange = {
256:             path: relativePath,
257:             status: "modified",
258:             timestamp: new Date(),
259:             ...await this.getFileInfo(sessionId, relativePath),
260:           };
261:           
262:           syncState.changes.set(relativePath, fileChange);
263:           changes.push(fileChange);
264:         } else {
265:           // File exists in both - check if different
266:           const originalChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(originalPath);
267:           const sessionChecksum = await this.calculateChecksum(sessionPath);
268:           const baselineChecksum = syncState.baselineChecksums.get(relativePath);
269:           
270:           if (originalChecksum !== sessionChecksum) {
271:             // Check if session file is modified by agent (differs from baseline)
272:             const sessionModified = baselineChecksum && sessionChecksum !== baselineChecksum;
273:             // Check if original file is modified
274:             const originalModified = baselineChecksum && originalChecksum !== baselineChecksum;
275:             
276:             if (sessionModified && originalModified) {
277:               // Conflict! Both changed
278:               const conflictChange: FileChange = {
279:                 path: relativePath,
280:                 status: "conflict",
281:                 timestamp: new Date(),
282:               };
283:               
284:               syncState.changes.set(relativePath, conflictChange);
285:               changes.push(conflictChange);
286:             } else {
287:               // Only original changed or only session changed (not both)
288:               // Copy from original to session
289:               copyFileSync(originalPath, sessionPath);
290:               
291:               // Update baseline
292:               syncState.baselineChecksums.set(relativePath, originalChecksum);
293:               
294:               const fileChange: FileChange = {
295:                 path: relativePath,
296:                 status: "modified",
297:                 timestamp: new Date(),
298:                 ...await this.getFileInfo(sessionId, relativePath),
299:               };
300:               
301:               syncState.changes.set(relativePath, fileChange);
302:               changes.push(fileChange);
303:             }
304:           }
305:         }
306:       }
307:     );
308: 
309:     syncState.lastSyncAt = new Date();
310:     return changes;
311:   }
312: 
313:   async resolveConflict(
314:     sessionId: string,
315:     filePath: string,
316:     resolution: "session" | "original" | "merge"
317:   ): Promise<void> {
318:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
319:     if (!syncState) {
320:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not initialized`);
321:     }
322: 
323:     const sessionPath = join(syncState.agentWorkspacePath, filePath);
324:     const originalPath = join(syncState.upstreamPath, filePath);
325: 
326:     if (resolution === "session") {
327:       // Keep session version
328:       if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
329:         const originalDir = dirname(originalPath);
330:         if (!existsSync(originalDir)) {
331:           mkdirSync(originalDir, { recursive: true });
332:         }
333:         copyFileSync(sessionPath, originalPath);
334:       }
335:     } else if (resolution === "original") {
336:       // Keep original version
337:       if (existsSync(originalPath)) {
338:         const sessionDir = dirname(sessionPath);
339:         if (!existsSync(sessionDir)) {
340:           mkdirSync(sessionDir, { recursive: true });
341:         }
342:         copyFileSync(originalPath, sessionPath);
343:       }
344:     }
345:     // "merge" would require a merge tool - not implemented yet
346: 
347:     // Update status to clean (no longer conflicting)
348:     const fileChange: FileChange = {
349:       path: filePath,
350:       status: "clean",
351:       timestamp: new Date(),
352:       ...await this.getFileInfo(sessionId, filePath),
353:     };
354: 
355:     syncState.changes.set(filePath, fileChange);
356:   }
357: 
358:   async getChangeSet(sessionId: string): Promise<ChangeSet> {
359:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
360:     if (!syncState) {
361:       return {
362:         sessionId,
363:         files: [],
364:         hasConflicts: false,
365:       };
366:     }
367: 
368:     const files = Array.from(syncState.changes.values());
369:     const hasConflicts = files.some(f => f.status === "conflict");
370: 
371:     return {
372:       sessionId,
373:       files: files.filter(f => f.status !== "clean"),
374:       hasConflicts,
375:       syncedAt: syncState.lastSyncAt,
376:     };
377:   }
378: 
379:   async getFileStatus(sessionId: string, filePath: string): Promise<FileStatus> {
380:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
381:     if (!syncState) return "clean";
382: 
383:     const change = syncState.changes.get(filePath);
384:     return change?.status || "clean";
385:   }
386: 
387:   async scanSessionCheckout(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
388:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
389:     if (!syncState) return;
390: 
391:     // First scan the original repo to establish baseline
392:     await this.scanDirectory(
393:       syncState.upstreamPath,
394:       syncState.upstreamPath,
395:       async (fullPath, relativePath) => {
396:         const checksum = await this.calculateChecksum(fullPath);
397:         syncState.baselineChecksums.set(relativePath, checksum);
398:       }
399:     );
400: 
401:     // Then scan session worktree
402:     await this.scanDirectory(
403:       syncState.agentWorkspacePath,
404:       syncState.agentWorkspacePath,
405:       async (fullPath, relativePath) => {
406:         const fileChange: FileChange = {
407:           path: relativePath,
408:           status: "clean",
409:           timestamp: new Date(),
410:           ...await this.getFileInfo(sessionId, relativePath),
411:         };
412: 
413:         syncState.changes.set(relativePath, fileChange);
414:       }
415:     );
416:   }
417: 
418:   private async scanDirectory(
419:     dirPath: string,
420:     basePath: string,
421:     callback: (fullPath: string, relativePath: string) => Promise<void>
422:   ): Promise<void> {
423:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
424: 
425:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
426:     
427:     for (const entry of entries) {
428:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
429:       const relativePath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
430: 
431:       // Skip hidden files and directories
432:       if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
433: 
434:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
435:         await this.scanDirectory(fullPath, basePath, callback);
436:       } else {
437:         await callback(fullPath, relativePath);
438:       }
439:     }
440:   }
441: 
442:   private async getFileInfo(sessionId: string, filePath: string): Promise<Partial<FileChange>> {
443:     const syncState = this.syncStates.get(sessionId);
444:     if (!syncState) return {};
445: 
446:     const sessionPath = join(syncState.agentWorkspacePath, filePath);
447:     
448:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
449:       return {};
450:     }
451: 
452:     const stats = statSync(sessionPath);
453:     const checksum = await this.calculateChecksum(sessionPath);
454: 
455:     return {
456:       size: stats.size,
457:       lastModified: stats.mtime,
458:       checksum,
459:     };
460:   }
461: 
462:   private async calculateChecksum(filePath: string): Promise<string> {
463:     const content = readFileSync(filePath);
464:     return crypto.createHash("md5").update(content).digest("hex");
465:   }
466: 
467:   async bufferChangesForReconnect(
468:     sessionId: string, 
469:     changes: FileChange[]
470:   ): Promise<void> {
471:     const buffered = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId) || [];
472:     this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, [...buffered, ...changes]);
473:   }
474: 
475:   async getBufferedChanges(sessionId: string): Promise<FileChange[]> {
476:     return this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId) || [];
477:   }
478: 
479:   async clearBufferedChanges(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
480:     this.pendingChanges.delete(sessionId);
481:   }
482: 
483:   async cleanupSession(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
484:     this.syncStates.delete(sessionId);
485:     this.pendingChanges.delete(sessionId);
486:   }
487: }
488: 
489: export const fileSyncService = new FileSyncService();

(End of file - total 489 lines)
</content>
```

#### Current State

You have a **3-buffer Emacs-style layout**:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│            Session Header               │
├────────────┬──────────────┬─────────────┤
│   Files    │     Chat     │   Changes   │
│   (Left)   │   (Center)   │   (Right)   │
│            │              │             │
│ File tree  │  Messages    │  Modified   │
│   view     │  + Input     │   files     │
└────────────┴──────────────┴─────────────┘
```

#### Your Vision

Replace "Files" with **"Impact"** - a shift from passive viewing to active understanding:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│            Session Header               │
├────────────┬──────────────┬─────────────┤
│   Impact   │     Chat     │   Changes   │
│   (Left)   │   (Center)   │   (Right)   │
├────────────┤              │             │
│ ┌────────┐ │              │  [M] file.ts│
│ │Fossil  │ │              │  [?] new.ts │
│ │  Web   │ │   Messages   │  [D] old.ts │
│ │ Link  ─┼─┼─▶           │             │
│ └────────┘ │              │             │
│ ┌────────┐ │              │             │
│ │ Impact │ │              │             │
│ │Metrics │ │              │             │
│ │ • New: │ │              │             │
│ │   5 ↑  │ │              │             │
│ │        │ │              │             │
│ │ • Chg: │ │              │             │
│ │   12 ↓ │ │              │             │
│ └────────┘ │              │             │
└────────────┴──────────────┴─────────────┘
```

## What Makes This Compelling

The **Impact** concept reframes the user's mental model:

| Before (Files) | After (Impact) |
|----------------|----------------|
| "What's in the workspace?" | "What have I done?" |
| Passive information | Active measurement |
| Just a file list | Story of the session's work |
| Static view | Dynamic comparison |

#### The Technical Shape

You need to compare **upstream/** vs **agent-workspace/**:

```
upstream/           agent-workspace/          Impact
─────────           ────────────────          ───────
file.ts  ─────┐                             
              ├──▶  file.ts (modified)   →   Changed: 1
new.ts        ┘                              New: 0 → 1 (+100%)

              ───▶  totally-new.ts        →   New: 1 → 2 (+100%)
              
old.ts   ─────┐                         →   Deleted: 1
              ├──▶  (gone)
              ┘
```

The **percentages** are interesting - they show *velocity* or *trend* over time. Are you accelerating or slowing down?

## Questions That Emerge

1. **Baseline for percentages**: Compared to what?
   - Last commit?
   - Session start?
   - Rolling window (last hour)?

2. **Fossil Web UI**: What does this look like?
   - Is it `fossil ui` running on a port?
   - A static file viewer?
   - Full diff browser?

3. **Real-time updates**: Does Impact refresh automatically as the agent works?

4. **The "Files" loss**: Do you ever need a simple file tree view? (Maybe as a toggle/modal?)

What resonates? What's the core story you're trying to tell with Impact?

## Clarified Requirements

| Aspect | Decision |
|--------|----------|
| **Buffers** | Only 2: Chat (center) + Impact (right) |
| **Baseline** | Compare `upstream/` vs `agent-workspace/` in real-time |
| **Fossil Link** | Link to running fossil server (already exists in session) |
| **Updates** | Auto-refresh as agent works |
| **Metrics** | Just counters: New, Changed, Deleted with arrows (trend vs previous state) |

#### The Architecture Question

How do we calculate "trend" (the ↑ ↓ → arrows)?

```
Option A: In-memory tracking
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  SyncService tracks previous counts    │
│  → Calculate delta in real-time        │
│  → Simple, no persistence needed       │
└────────────────────────────────────────┘

Option B: Time-based snapshots
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Compare current vs N minutes ago      │
│  → Needs timestamped snapshots         │
│  → More complex, shows velocity        │
└────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

Given you want minimal, **Option A** feels right - track previous scan results in memory, show delta.

#### The Data Flow

```
Agent writes file ──▶ FileWatcher detects ──▶ SyncService updates counts
                                                       │
                                                       ▼
                              ┌───────────────────────────────┐
                              │    ImpactCalculator (new)     │
                              │  • Scan upstream/             │
                              │  • Scan agent-workspace/      │
                              │  • Compare → counts           │
                              │  • Delta vs last scan         │
                              └───────────────┬───────────────┘
                                              │
                                              ▼
                              ┌───────────────────────────────┐
                              │     SessionDetailPage         │
                              │  ┌─────────────────────────────┐│
                              │  │        Impact Buffer      ││
                              │  │  ┌─────────────────┐      ││
                              │  │  │ Fossil Web Link │      ││
                              │  │  └─────────────────┘      ││
                              │  │                             ││
                              │  │  New:     5  ↑              ││
                              │  │  Changed: 12 ↓              ││
                              │  │  Deleted: 0  →              ││
                              │  │                             ││
                              │  └─────────────────────────────┘│
                              └───────────────────────────────┘
```

#### Open Questions

1. **Refresh interval**: How often? 5 seconds? On file change events?

2. **The ↑ ↓ → logic**:
   - ↑ = More than last scan (increasing)
   - ↓ = Less than last scan (decreasing - e.g., files committed)
   - → = Same as last scan

3. **Fossil server URL**: Is it `http://localhost:{port}/timeline` or just the root?

4. **Do you want to keep the "Commit" button** somewhere? Header bar?

What's your preference on refresh strategy and where the commit button lives?

```
└─────────────────────────────┴───────────────────────────────┘
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  [Commit]  [Settings]                    [Delete Session]   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**Impact Calculation:**
- Scan `upstream/` → baseline file list + checksums
- Scan `agent-workspace/` → current file list + checksums
- Compare:
  - **New**: In workspace, not in upstream
  - **Changed**: In both, different checksum
  - **Deleted**: In upstream, not in workspace

**Trend Tracking (in-memory):**
```typescript
interface ImpactState {
  newCount: number;
  changedCount: number;
  deletedCount: number;
  lastScanAt: Date;
}

// Compare with previous state to determine arrow
// ↑ = current > previous
// ↓ = current < previous  
// → = current === previous
```

**Auto-refresh:**
- Client-side polling every 5 seconds
- Endpoint: `GET /sessions/:id/impact`
- Returns: `{ new: 3, changed: 7, deleted: 0, trends: { new: "up", changed: "same", deleted: "same" } }`

Ready to start implementation with `/opsx:new` or `/opsx:ff`? Or any adjustments to the plan?

```
   ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────┐    ┌────────────┐
   │  Sync    │   │  Push    │    │   Impact   │
   │ Changes  │   │ to Repo  │    │   Store    │
   │          │   │          │    │            │
   └──────────┘   └──────────┘    │  Capture   │
```

#### Data Model

```typescript
// Stored on every commit
interface ImpactRecord {
  id: string;           // UUID
  sessionId: string;  // FK to session
  projectId: string;    // FK to project (denormalized for easy querying)
  commitHash: string;   // The fossil commit hash
  newCount: number;
  changedCount: number;
  deletedCount: number;
  totalFilesAtCommit: number;  // Context: how big was the codebase
  createdAt: Date;
}

// Relationship: Project 1:N ImpactRecords
// Can group by session for per-session history
```

#### Storage Options

Given the existing architecture uses YAML files in `~/.mimo/`:

```
~/.mimo/
└── projects/
    └── {project-id}/
        ├── impacts/
        │   └── {impact-id}.yaml     # Or single impacts.yaml array
        └── sessions/
            └── {session-id}/
                ├── session.yaml
                └── impacts.yaml     # Alternative: per-session
```

**Which feels right?**
- **A**: One `impacts/` folder per project (easy to query all project impacts)
- **B**: One `impacts.yaml` per session (deletes with session, but you said you want to keep them even if session deleted)

So **A** is the answer - project-level storage, survives session deletion.

## Questions

1. **Impact ID**: Use timestamp? UUID? `sessionId-commitHash` composite?

2. **Session link**: Do you want to see session name in history even if session deleted? (We'd need to denormalize/dup the name at commit time)

3. **Commit message**: Store it too? (Useful for context)

4. **Fossil timeline link**: Link each commit to fossil web view?

What resonates?

This adds more depth to the Impact feature. Let me think through this:

The impact calculation now becomes:
- File counts (new/changed/deleted)
- Lines of code (added/removed)
- Complexity (increased/decreased)

scc can analyze code and provide these metrics. The workflow would be:
1. Run scc on upstream/ → baseline metrics
2. Run scc on agent-workspace/ → current metrics
3. Compare to get deltas

```
│                                                             │
│  [View Full scc Report]                                     │
│                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### The scc Integration

**Auto-install:**
```typescript
// Check on startup
if (!sccInstalled()) {
  await installScc(); // Download from GitHub releases
}
```

**Metrics from scc:**
- `--by-file` - Get per-file stats
- `- complexity` - Cyclomatic complexity
- `- code` - Lines of code
- `--format json` - Parseable output

**Complexity Comparison:**
```
upstream/               agent-workspace/
───────────             ────────────────
scc --by-file           scc --by-file
┌─────────┐             ┌─────────┐
│foo.ts   │             │foo.ts   │
│ C: 5    │             │ C: 8    │  → Changed, +3 complexity
│ LOC: 45 │             │ LOC: 52 │  → +7 lines
└─────────┘             └─────────┘

new.ts                  → New file, add full metrics
old.ts (deleted)        → Removed, subtract metrics
```

## Storage Model (Updated)

```typescript
// ~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/{sessionId-commitHash}.yaml

id: "abc123-def456"
sessionId: "abc123"
sessionName: "feature-auth"  // Denormalized for display
projectId: "proj789"
commitHash: "def456"
commitDate: "2024-01-15T14:30:00Z"

// File counts
files:
  new: 3
  changed: 7
  deleted: 0

// Lines of code (from scc)
linesOfCode:
  added: 245
  removed: 12
  net: 233

// Complexity (from scc)
complexity:
  cyclomatic: 18      // Total cyclomatic complexity
  cognitive: 5        // Cognitive complexity (if available)
  estimatedMinutes: 120  // scc time estimate
  byLanguage:         // Breakdown if useful
    typescript:
      files: 8
      loc: 233
      complexity: 18

// Links
fossilUrl: "http://localhost:8080/timeline?c=def456"
```

#### The Implementation Layers

```
Layer 1: scc Service
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│  • Auto-download scc binary         │
│  • Run on directory                 │
│  • Parse JSON output                │
│  • Cache results (5s TTL)           │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
              │
              ▼
Layer 2: Impact Calculator
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│  • Scan both directories            │
│  • Run scc on each                  │
│  • Calculate deltas                 │
│  • Track trends vs previous         │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
              │
              ▼
Layer 3: API + UI
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│  • /sessions/:id/impact endpoint    │
│  • Impact buffer component          │
│  • 5s polling from client           │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
              │
              ▼
Layer 4: Persistence
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│  • Save on commit                   │
│  • Impact history page              │
│  • Session linking logic            │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Questions

1. **scc install location**: `~/.mimo/bin/scc` or system-wide?

4. **scc cache**: Cache metrics for 5s to avoid re-running constantly?

5. **Error handling**: If scc fails, show file counts only with warning?

````
<skill_content name="openspec-ff-change">
# Skill: openspec-ff-change

Fast-forward through artifact creation - generate everything needed to start implementation in one go.

**Input**: The user's request should include a change name (kebab-case) OR a description of what they want to build.

**Steps**

1. **If no clear input provided, ask what they want to build**

   Use the **AskUserQuestion tool** (open-ended, no preset options) to ask:
   > "What change do you want to work on? Describe what you want to build or fix."

   From their description, derive a kebab-case name (e.g., "add user authentication" → `add-user-auth`).

   **IMPORTANT**: Do NOT proceed without understanding what the user wants to build.

2. **Create the change directory**
   ```bash
   openspec new change "<name>"
   ```
   This creates a scaffolded change at `openspec/changes/<name>/`.

3. **Get the artifact build order**
   ```bash
   openspec status --change "<name>" --json
   ```
   Parse the JSON to get:
   - `applyRequires`: array of artifact IDs needed before implementation (e.g., `["tasks"]`)
   - `artifacts`: list of all artifacts with their status and dependencies

4. **Create artifacts in sequence until apply-ready**

   Use the **TodoWrite tool** to track progress through the artifacts.

   Loop through artifacts in dependency order (artifacts with no pending dependencies first):

   a. **For each artifact that is `ready` (dependencies satisfied)**:
      - Get instructions:
        ```bash
        openspec instructions <artifact-id> --change "<name>" --json
        ```
      - The instructions JSON includes:
        - `context`: Project background (constraints for you - do NOT include in output)
        - `rules`: Artifact-specific rules (constraints for you - do NOT include in output)
        - `template`: The structure to use for your output file
        - `instruction`: Schema-specific guidance for this artifact type
        - `outputPath`: Where to write the artifact
        - `dependencies`: Completed artifacts to read for context
      - Read any completed dependency files for context
      - Create the artifact file using `template` as the structure
      - Apply `context` and `rules` as constraints - but do NOT copy them into the file
      - Show brief progress: "✓ Created <artifact-id>"

   b. **Continue until all `applyRequires` artifacts are complete**
      - After creating each artifact, re-run `openspec status --change "<name>" --json`
      - Check if every artifact ID in `applyRequires` has `status: "done"` in the artifacts array
      - Stop when all `applyRequires` artifacts are done

   c. **If an artifact requires user input** (unclear context):
      - Use **AskUserQuestion tool** to clarify
      - Then continue with creation

5. **Show final status**
   ```bash
   openspec status --change "<name>"
   ```

**Output**

After completing all artifacts, summarize:
- Change name and location
- List of artifacts created with brief descriptions
- What's ready: "All artifacts created! Ready for implementation."
- Prompt: "Run `/opsx:apply` or ask me to implement to start working on the tasks."

**Artifact Creation Guidelines**

- Follow the `instruction` field from `openspec instructions` for each artifact type
- The schema defines what each artifact should contain - follow it
- Read dependency artifacts for context before creating new ones
- Use `template` as the structure for your output file - fill in its sections
- **IMPORTANT**: `context` and `rules` are constraints for YOU, not content for the file
  - Do NOT copy `<context>`, `<rules>`, `<project_context>` blocks into the artifact
  - These guide what you write, but should never appear in the output

**Guardrails**
- Create ALL artifacts needed for implementation (as defined by schema's `apply.requires`)
- Always read dependency artifacts before creating a new one
- If context is critically unclear, ask the user - but prefer making reasonable decisions to keep momentum
- If a change with that name already exists, suggest continuing that change instead
- Verify each artifact file exists after writing before proceeding to next

Base directory for this skill: file:///home/bit4bit/src/mimo/.opencode/skills/openspec-ff-change
Relative paths in this skill (e.g., scripts/, reference/) are relative to this base directory.
Note: file list is sampled.

<skill_files>

</skill_files>
</skill_content>
````

Why now?\n- **What Changes**: Bullet list of changes. Be specific about new capabilities, modifications, or removals. Mark breaking changes with **BREAKING**.\n- **Capabilities**: Identify which specs will be created or modified:\n  - **New Capabilities**: List capabilities being introduced. Each becomes a new `specs/<name>/spec.md`. Use kebab-case names (e.g., `user-auth`, `data-export`).\n  - **Modified Capabilities**: List existing capabilities whose REQUIREMENTS are changing. Only include if spec-level behavior changes (not just implementation details). Each needs a delta spec file. Check `openspec/specs/` for existing spec names. Leave empty if no requirement changes.\n- **Impact**: Affected code, APIs, dependencies, or systems.\n\nIMPORTANT: The Capabilities section is critical. It creates the contract between\nproposal and specs phases. Research existing specs before filling this in.\nEach capability listed here will need a corresponding spec file.\n\nKeep it concise (1-2 pages). Focus on the \"why\" not the \"how\" -\nimplementation details belong in design.md.\n\nThis is the foundation - specs, design, and tasks all build on this.\n",
```
  "template": "## Why\n\n<!-- Explain the motivation for this change. What problem does this solve? Why now? -->\n\n## What Changes\n\n<!-- Describe what will change. Be specific about new capabilities, modifications, or removals. -->\n\n## Capabilities\n\n### New Capabilities\n<!-- Capabilities being introduced. Replace <name> with kebab-case identifier (e.g., user-auth, data-export, api-rate-limiting). Each creates specs/<name>/spec.md -->\n- `<name>`: <brief description of what this capability covers>\n\n### Modified Capabilities\n<!-- Existing capabilities whose REQUIREMENTS are changing (not just implementation).\n     Only list here if spec-level behavior changes. Each needs a delta spec file.\n     Use existing spec names from openspec/specs/. Leave empty if no requirement changes. -->\n- `<existing-name>`: <what requirement is changing>\n\n## Impact\n\n<!-- Affected code, APIs, dependencies, systems -->\n",
  "dependencies": [],
  "unlocks": [
    "design",
    "specs"
  ]
}
```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-06 21:40:17)

Now I'll create the proposal.md file following the template and instructions.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/proposal.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:40:28
**Parameters:**
content: ## Why

The current session view shows a "Changes" buffer that simply lists modified files, but doesn't tell the story of the work being done. Users need visibility into the actual impact of their agent's work - not just what changed, but how much code was affected, how complex it is, and the velocity of changes. This insight helps users understand the scope and risk of commits before pushing.

## What Changes

- **Replace Changes buffer with Impact buffer**: Remove the passive file list from the right buffer; keep only Chat (center) and Impact (right) buffers
- **Real-time impact metrics**: Show new/changed/deleted file counts with trend indicators (↑ ↓ →)
- **Lines of Code tracking**: Display added, removed, and net LOC changes
- **Code complexity analysis**: Integrate scc (Sloc Cloc and Code) to show cyclomatic complexity, cognitive complexity, and estimated time per change
- **Language breakdown**: Show metrics grouped by programming language
- **Per-file complexity detail**: Expandable view showing individual file complexity metrics
- **Auto-install scc**: Download and install scc binary to `~/.mimo/bin/scc` automatically
- **Impact persistence**: Store impact metrics on every commit at `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/{sessionId-commitHash}.yaml`
- **Impact history page**: New page showing all impacts for a project with session links, commit hashes, and full metrics
- **Fossil integration**: Link to fossil web UI (timeline, diff, files) in Impact buffer
- **5-second polling**: Auto-refresh metrics in real-time as agent works

## Capabilities

### New Capabilities
- `impact-tracking`: Real-time and historical tracking of code change impact including file counts, LOC, and complexity metrics
- `scc-integration`: Automatic installation and execution of scc for code complexity analysis
- `impact-history`: Persistence and retrieval of impact records per project with session correlation

### Modified Capabilities
- `session-ui`: Modify SessionDetailPage to replace Changes buffer with Impact buffer (2-buffer layout)

## Impact

- **SessionDetailPage.tsx**: Major UI restructuring - remove Changes buffer, add Impact buffer
- **sync/service.ts**: Extend FileSyncService with impact calculation
- **New services**: scc service, impact calculator, impact repository
- **New routes**: Impact metrics API endpoint, impact history page
- **New components**: ImpactBuffer component, ImpactHistoryPage component
- **Dependencies**: scc binary (auto-downloaded), fossil web server (existing)

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/proposal.md

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-06 21:40:41)

Let me create the design document first, then create the spec files for the three new capabilities.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/design.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:40:56
**Parameters:**
content: ## Context

The current SessionDetailPage shows three buffers: Files (left), Chat (center), and Changes (right). The Changes buffer only lists modified files without providing insight into the scope, complexity, or velocity of work. Users need to understand not just WHAT changed, but HOW MUCH changed, HOW COMPLEX it is, and at what VELOCITY.

The system already has:
- FileSyncService that tracks file changes between upstream/ and agent-workspace/
- Fossil integration for VCS operations
- Session infrastructure with chat and agent management

## Goals / Non-Goals

**Goals:**
- Replace the passive Changes buffer with an active Impact buffer
- Show real-time file count metrics (new/changed/deleted) with trend indicators
- Track lines of code (added/removed/net) changes
- Integrate scc for code complexity analysis (cyclomatic, cognitive, estimated time)
- Display language-specific breakdowns of metrics
- Provide per-file complexity detail (expandable)
- Auto-install scc dependency
- Persist impact metrics on commit to `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/`
- Create impact history page for project-wide view
- Maintain 5-second polling for real-time updates

**Non-Goals:**
- Historical trending graphs (sparklines over time)
- Diff viewer integration (only link to fossil)
- Git complexity support (scc handles both)
- Configurable polling intervals
- Impact export/download functionality

## Decisions

### Decision: Two-buffer layout (Chat + Impact)
**Rationale**: The Files buffer was redundant - users can explore files via the file tree dialog. The Impact buffer provides actionable intelligence that Changes never could.

**Alternatives considered**:
- Keep 3 buffers (Files, Chat, Impact) - rejected: too crowded
- Replace Files instead of Changes - rejected: Impact relates to Changes, not file browsing

### Decision: Auto-install scc to ~/.mimo/bin/scc
**Rationale**: scc is a compiled Go binary. Rather than requiring manual installation or Docker, we download the appropriate binary for the platform on first use.

**Download source**: GitHub releases (https://github.com/boyter/scc/releases)
**Platform detection**: Runtime detection of OS/arch

### Decision: In-memory trend tracking
**Rationale**: Trend arrows (↑ ↓ →) compare current scan vs previous scan in memory. No persistence needed - trends are ephemeral indicators of velocity.

**Trade-off**: Trends reset on server restart, but this is acceptable for velocity indicators.

### Decision: Impact record stored on commit, not continuously
**Rationale**: Only the commit matters for history. Continuous snapshotting would create noise.

**Storage path**: `~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/{sessionId-commitHash}.yaml`

### Decision: Composite key for impact records
**Rationale**: `sessionId-commitHash` ensures uniqueness while maintaining session correlation. Session can be deleted but impact record survives.

### Decision: scc 5-second cache per session
**Rationale**: Running scc is expensive (disk I/O). Cache results for 5 seconds to avoid hammering the filesystem while maintaining near-real-time feel.

### Decision: Show "scc not installed" warning with install button
**Rationale**: If auto-install fails (network, permissions), user can manually trigger. Fallback to file counts only.

## Risks / Trade-offs

**[Risk]** scc binary download fails or is blocked by corporate proxy
→ **Mitigation**: Clear error message with manual download instructions; fallback to file-only metrics

**[Risk]** scc scanning large repositories causes performance issues
→ **Mitigation**: 5-second cache reduces scan frequency; consider adding scan timeout (30s)

**[Risk]** Impact history YAML files accumulate over time
→ **Mitigation**: YAML is compact; can implement cleanup/archive later if needed

**[Risk]** Complexity metrics confuse non-technical users
→ **Mitigation**: Make per-file detail collapsed by default; show tooltips explaining metrics

**[Trade-off]** Denormalized sessionName in impact records
We store sessionName at commit time so history shows meaningful names even if session deleted. This creates minor data duplication but improves UX significantly.

## Migration Plan

**No breaking changes** - this is purely additive:
1. Deploy new services (SccService, ImpactCalculator, ImpactRepository)
2. Deploy modified SessionDetailPage (2-buffer layout)
3. Existing sessions continue working; Impact buffer shows on next load
4. scc auto-installs on first metrics request

**Rollback**: Revert to previous commit; Impact buffer disappears, Changes buffer returns

## Open Questions

1. Should we set a maximum scan timeout for scc on very large repos?
2. Should complexity trends show "+18" or "+18 from +12" (previous absolute)?
3. Do we need a "Clear History" button on the impact history page?

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/design.md


## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-06 21:41:24)

Now I'll create the three spec files. Let me start with impact-tracking, then scc-integration, then impact-history.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/impact-tracking/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:42:06
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Real-time impact metrics
The system SHALL calculate and display file impact metrics in real-time, comparing agent-workspace against upstream.

#### Scenario: Calculate file counts
- **WHEN** the Impact buffer is loaded or refreshed
- **THEN** the system SHALL scan both upstream/ and agent-workspace/ directories
- **AND** calculate new files (in workspace, not in upstream)
- **AND** calculate changed files (in both, different checksum)
- **AND** calculate deleted files (in upstream, not in workspace)

### Requirement: Trend indicators
The system SHALL display trend indicators (↑ ↓ →) showing velocity of changes compared to previous scan.

#### Scenario: Show increasing trend
- **WHEN** new file count increases from previous scan
- **THEN** display "↑" indicator next to new file count

#### Scenario: Show decreasing trend
- **WHEN** changed file count decreases from previous scan
- **THEN** display "↓" indicator next to changed file count

#### Scenario: Show stable trend
- **WHEN** deleted file count matches previous scan
- **THEN** display "→" indicator next to deleted file count

### Requirement: Lines of Code tracking
The system SHALL track lines of code changes between upstream and agent-workspace.

#### Scenario: Calculate LOC metrics
- **WHEN** the Impact buffer displays metrics
- **THEN** show total lines added (new + modified additions)
- **AND** show total lines removed (deleted + modified removals)
- **AND** show net LOC change (added - removed)
- **AND** display trend indicators for each metric

### Requirement: 5-second polling
The system SHALL auto-refresh impact metrics every 5 seconds while the session page is active.

#### Scenario: Poll for updates
- **WHEN** user is on the session detail page
- **THEN** the client SHALL poll /sessions/:id/impact every 5 seconds
- **AND** update the Impact buffer with fresh metrics

### Requirement: Two-buffer layout
The system SHALL display only Chat (center) and Impact (right) buffers, removing the Changes buffer.

#### Scenario: View session detail
- **WHEN** user navigates to a session detail page
- **THEN** display the Chat buffer in the center
- **AND** display the Impact buffer on the right
- **AND** the Changes buffer SHALL NOT be visible

### Requirement: Fossil web integration
The system SHALL provide links to the fossil web interface for the current session.

#### Scenario: View fossil timeline
- **WHEN** user clicks "Timeline" link in Impact buffer
- **THEN** open fossil web timeline in a new tab

#### Scenario: View fossil diff
- **WHEN** user clicks "Diff" link in Impact buffer
- **THEN** open fossil web diff view in a new tab

#### Scenario: View fossil files
- **WHEN** user clicks "Files" link in Impact buffer
- **THEN** open fossil web file browser in a new tab

## MODIFIED Requirements

### Requirement: Session UI displays buffers
The SessionDetailPage SHALL display the Chat buffer and Impact buffer.

#### Scenario: Render session detail
- **WHEN** the system renders the SessionDetailPage
- **THEN** the Chat buffer SHALL occupy the center position
- **AND** the Impact buffer SHALL occupy the right position
- **AND** no Changes buffer SHALL be rendered

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/impact-tracking/spec.md

```

@@ -0,0 +1,79 @@
+## ADDED Requirements
+
+### Requirement: Real-time impact metrics
+The system SHALL calculate and display file impact metrics in real-time, comparing agent-workspace against upstream.
+
+#### Scenario: Calculate file counts
+- **WHEN** the Impact buffer is loaded or refreshed
+- **THEN** the system SHALL scan both upstream/ and agent-workspace/ directories
+- **AND** calculate new files (in workspace, not in upstream)
+- **AND** calculate changed files (in both, different checksum)
+- **AND** calculate deleted files (in upstream, not in workspace)
+
+### Requirement: Trend indicators
+The system SHALL display trend indicators (↑ ↓ →) showing velocity of changes compared to previous scan.
+
+#### Scenario: Show increasing trend
+- **WHEN** new file count increases from previous scan
+- **THEN** display "↑" indicator next to new file count
+
+#### Scenario: Show decreasing trend
+- **WHEN** changed file count decreases from previous scan
+- **THEN** display "↓" indicator next to changed file count
+
+#### Scenario: Show stable trend
+- **WHEN** deleted file count matches previous scan
+- **THEN** display "→" indicator next to deleted file count
+
+### Requirement: Lines of Code tracking
+The system SHALL track lines of code changes between upstream and agent-workspace.
+
+#### Scenario: Calculate LOC metrics
+- **WHEN** the Impact buffer displays metrics
+- **THEN** show total lines added (new + modified additions)
+- **AND** show total lines removed (deleted + modified removals)
+- **AND** show net LOC change (added - removed)
+- **AND** display trend indicators for each metric
+
+### Requirement: 5-second polling
+The system SHALL auto-refresh impact metrics every 5 seconds while the session page is active.
+
+#### Scenario: Poll for updates
+- **WHEN** user is on the session detail page
+- **THEN** the client SHALL poll /sessions/:id/impact every 5 seconds
+- **AND** update the Impact buffer with fresh metrics
+
+### Requirement: Two-buffer layout
+The system SHALL display only Chat (center) and Impact (right) buffers, removing the Changes buffer.
+
+#### Scenario: View session detail
+- **WHEN** user navigates to a session detail page
+- **THEN** display the Chat buffer in the center
+- **AND** display the Impact buffer on the right
+- **AND** the Changes buffer SHALL NOT be visible
+
+### Requirement: Fossil web integration
+The system SHALL provide links to the fossil web interface for the current session.
+
+#### Scenario: View fossil timeline
+- **WHEN** user clicks "Timeline" link in Impact buffer
+- **THEN** open fossil web timeline in a new tab
+
+#### Scenario: View fossil diff
+- **WHEN** user clicks "Diff" link in Impact buffer
+- **THEN** open fossil web diff view in a new tab
+
+#### Scenario: View fossil files
+- **WHEN** user clicks "Files" link in Impact buffer
+- **THEN** open fossil web file browser in a new tab
+
+## MODIFIED Requirements
+
+### Requirement: Session UI displays buffers
+The SessionDetailPage SHALL display the Chat buffer and Impact buffer.
+
+#### Scenario: Render session detail
+- **WHEN** the system renders the SessionDetailPage
+- **THEN** the Chat buffer SHALL occupy the center position
+- **AND** the Impact buffer SHALL occupy the right position
+- **AND** no Changes buffer SHALL be rendered
```


### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/scc-integration/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:42:06
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/scc-integration/spec.md
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Automatic scc installation
The system SHALL automatically download and install the scc binary when first needed.

#### Scenario: First metrics request
- **WHEN** impact metrics are requested and scc is not installed
- **THEN** detect the current platform (OS/architecture)
- **AND** download appropriate scc release from GitHub
- **AND** install to ~/.mimo/bin/scc
- **AND** make executable

#### Scenario: scc already installed
- **WHEN** impact metrics are requested and scc exists at ~/.mimo/bin/scc
- **THEN** skip download and use existing binary

### Requirement: scc execution
The system SHALL execute scc on directories to extract complexity metrics.

#### Scenario: Run scc on workspace
- **WHEN** calculating impact metrics
- **THEN** execute scc --by-file --format json on agent-workspace/
- **AND** execute scc --by-file --format json on upstream/
- **AND** parse JSON output for metrics

### Requirement: Complexity metrics extraction
The system SHALL extract code complexity metrics from scc output.

#### Scenario: Parse cyclomatic complexity
- **WHEN** scc JSON output is received
- **THEN** extract cyclomatic complexity per file
- **AND** calculate total complexity delta

#### Scenario: Parse cognitive complexity
- **WHEN** scc JSON output includes cognitive complexity
- **THEN** extract cognitive complexity per file
- **AND** calculate total cognitive complexity delta

#### Scenario: Parse estimated time
- **WHEN** scc JSON output includes estimated time
- **THEN** extract estimated development time per file
- **AND** calculate total estimated time delta

### Requirement: Language breakdown
The system SHALL group metrics by programming language.

#### Scenario: Display language metrics
- **WHEN** displaying complexity metrics
- **THEN** show metrics grouped by language (e.g., TypeScript, Python)
- **AND** for each language show: file count, LOC, complexity

### Requirement: Per-file complexity detail
The system SHALL provide expandable per-file complexity details.

#### Scenario: View file details
- **WHEN** user expands a file in the complexity section
- **THEN** show: file path, LOC, cyclomatic complexity, cognitive complexity
- **AND** indicate if file is new, changed, or deleted

### Requirement: scc result caching
The system SHALL cache scc results for 5 seconds to avoid repeated scanning.

#### Scenario: Cache hit
- **WHEN** impact metrics are requested within 5 seconds of previous request
- **THEN** return cached scc results
- **AND** do not re-execute scc

#### Scenario: Cache miss
- **WHEN** impact metrics are requested and cache is expired
- **THEN** execute scc
- **AND** store results in cache with 5-second TTL

### Requirement: scc error handling
The system SHALL handle scc failures gracefully.

#### Scenario: scc not installed and download fails
- **WHEN** scc is needed but not installed and download fails
- **THEN** display warning: "scc not available - showing file counts only"
- **AND** show [Install scc] button for manual retry
- **AND** continue with file count metrics (no complexity)

#### Scenario: scc execution timeout
- **WHEN** scc execution exceeds 30 seconds
- **THEN** cancel the scan
- **AND** display warning: "scc scan timed out - showing file counts only"
- **AND** continue with file count metrics



### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/impact-history/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-06 21:42:06
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Impact record creation on commit
The system SHALL create an impact record on every commit, storing the current metrics.

#### Scenario: Commit triggers impact storage
- **WHEN** user clicks Commit button and commit succeeds
- **THEN** capture current file counts (new/changed/deleted)
- **AND** capture current LOC metrics
- **AND** capture current complexity metrics
- **AND** store to ~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/{sessionId-commitHash}.yaml

### Requirement: Impact record data structure
The system SHALL store specific fields in each impact record.

#### Scenario: Store impact metadata
- **WHEN** creating an impact record
- **THEN** include: id, sessionId, sessionName, projectId, commitHash, commitDate
- **AND** include files: {new, changed, deleted}
- **AND** include linesOfCode: {added, removed, net}
- **AND** include complexity: {cyclomatic, cognitive, estimatedMinutes}
- **AND** include complexityByLanguage: array of language breakdowns
- **AND** include fossilUrl for viewing commit

### Requirement: Impact record survives session deletion
The system SHALL retain impact records even if the associated session is deleted.

#### Scenario: View impact of deleted session
- **WHEN** viewing impact history and session has been deleted
- **THEN** display impact record normally
- **AND** show "(session deleted)" indicator
- **AND** do not link to session detail

### Requirement: Project impact history page
The system SHALL provide a page listing all impact records for a project.

#### Scenario: View project history
- **WHEN** user navigates to /projects/{id}/impacts
- **THEN** display table of all impact records for the project
- **AND** sort by commitDate descending (newest first)
- **AND** show: session name, commit hash, files, LOC, complexity, date

#### Scenario: Session link in history
- **WHEN** impact record has an existing session
- **THEN** session name SHALL be a link to /sessions/{sessionId}
- **AND** link SHALL open in new tab

#### Scenario: Deleted session in history
- **WHEN** impact record references a deleted session
- **THEN** display session name with "(deleted)" suffix
- **AND** no link SHALL be rendered

### Requirement: Fossil commit links
The system SHALL provide links to fossil web for each commit in the history.

#### Scenario: View commit in fossil
- **WHEN** user clicks commit hash in impact history
- **THEN** open fossil web timeline/diff for that commit in new tab

### Requirement: Composite key storage
The system SHALL use sessionId-commitHash as the filename for impact records.

#### Scenario: Store with composite key
- **WHEN** persisting an impact record
- **THEN** filename SHALL be {sessionId}-{commitHash}.yaml
- **AND** directory SHALL be ~/.mimo/projects/{project-id}/impacts/

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/add-impact-buffer/specs/impact-history/spec.md

```
4: The system SHALL allow users to create sessions within a project. Each session creates repo.fossil but defers checkout creation to agent bootstrap.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Create session with title
7: - **WHEN** authenticated user submits session title "fix-auth-bug" for project "my-app"
8: - **THEN** system creates directory ~/.mimo/projects/my-app/sessions/fix-auth-bug/

12: - **AND** system displays session view
13:

15: - **WHEN** session is created
16: - **THEN** system stores port: null in session.yaml
17: - **AND** fossil server is NOT started at creation time
18: - **AND** port is assigned when agent connects (see agent-lifecycle)
19:

21: - **WHEN** user submits session title that already exists in project
22: - **THEN** system appends timestamp to title or returns error
23:

25: The system SHALL allow users to remove sessions.
26:

28: - **WHEN** authenticated user deletes session "fix-auth-bug"

30: - **AND** system stops Fossil server if running
31: - **AND** system removes entire session directory including checkout/ and repo.fossil
32: 
33: ## REMOVED Requirements
34: 
35: ### Requirement: System starts Fossil server on session creation
36: **Reason**: Fossil server now starts when agent connects, not at session creation. This enables deferred bootstrap where agent creates the checkout.
```
